# non-hangul-codes.txt (Version 09/07/95)
#
# 	This file was created by Ken Lunde of Adobe Systems
# Incorporated (lunde@mv.us.adobe.com), and provides mappings for the
# 5,874 non-hangul characters in KS C 5601-1992 (4,888 hanja and 986
# symbols). Anyone is hereby permitted to use and redistribute this
# file for non-commercial purposes as long as its contents are
# unmodified.
# 	The three fields, all tab-delimited, represent the following
# encodings:
#
# o KS C 5601-1992 (7-bit ISO 2022) Code
# o Wansung Code (the code points for these 5,874 characters are
#   identical to Microsoft's Unified Hangul Code)
# o Johab (described in KS C 5601-1992)
#
# 	The master URL of this document is:
#
#   ftp://ftp.ora.com/pub/examples/nutshell/ujip/map/non-hangul-codes.txt
#
# The following file provides mappings for the 11,172 pre-combined
# hangul characters of KS C 5601-1992:
#
#   ftp://unicode.org/pub/MappingTables/EastAsiaMaps/hangul-codes.txt
#
# KS	Wansung	Johab
# ======================
